  I just made minor changes for self-understanding. I don't claim authority of any class.

Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2972" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2977" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2983" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2987" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4641" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4654" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4656" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4657" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4659" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1114" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4665" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4667" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4670" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4674" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4675" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4677" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4687" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4723" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4739" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1214" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4749" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4752" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1214" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4760" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4762" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4769" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4809" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4822" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4825" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4827" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1214" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4833" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4835" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4855" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6778" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6783" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6791" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6793" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6797" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6805" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6805" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6818" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6783" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6835" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6873" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6880" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6886" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6783" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6903" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10454" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10495" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10521" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10546" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10587" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10616" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10689" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10696" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10707" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12065" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="12070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12070" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="12079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12081" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12085" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="12093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12093" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="12101" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12103" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12104" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="12107" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12112" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12114" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11041" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="12123" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12125" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12126" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="12129" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12131" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4067" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12134" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12136" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12070" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="12148" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12346" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12346" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12355" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#997" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12363" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2497" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12369" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12070" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15278" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15282" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15294" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15298" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16767" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="17031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17031" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="17041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3835" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="17048" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17050" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="17055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12070" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17320" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17327" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17327" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17333" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18224" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
